kell0rskaiiiter!~ev0l@p41nz.users.quakenet.org #cyberscripters blueyonder1.uk.quakenet.org QuakeNet alias treeview { var %dn,%did,%sel,%root,%line,%text | if ($0 == 1) { %dn = $dname | %did = $1 } | else { %dn = $1 | %did = $2 } | %sel = $gettok($did(%dn,%did,1),3-,32) | %root = root $gettok(%sel,2-,32) up | %line = $gettok(%sel,-1,32) | did -i %dn %did 1 cb %root | %text = $did(%dn,%did,%line) | if ($prop == text) { return $gettok(%text,7-,32) } }
